JOIN `sp_order` as `c` ON `a`.`order_id` = `c`.`order_id`
JOIN `sp_user` as `b` ON `c`.`user_id`=`b`.`id`
JOIN `sp_invoice_stat` as `d` ON `a`.`istat_code` = `d`.`istat_code`
JOIN `sp_number` as `e` ON `a`.`number_id`=`e`.`number_id`
JOIN `sp_p_product` as `f` ON `a`.`product_id`=`f`.`product_id`
JOIN `sp_order_type` as `g` ON `c`.`otype_code`=`g`.`otype_code`
JOIN `sp_provider` as `h` ON `h`.`provider_id`=`f`.`provider_id`
WHERE `a`.`invoice_id` = '739'
ORDER BY `a`.`invoice_date` DESC 
 Execution Time:7.1048736572266E-5

WHERE `c`.`invoice_number` = '0516/INV/PS/MEI/2016'

SELECT `sp_user_mod`.`ul_id` as `id`, `sp_user_level`.`name`, `sp_user_level`.`description`
FROM `sp_user_mod`
JOIN `sp_user_level` ON `sp_user_mod`.`ul_id`=`sp_user_level`.`id`
WHERE `sp_user_mod`.`user_id` = '2' 
 Execution Time:0.00018405914306641

SELECT *
FROM `sp_invoice` as `a`
JOIN `sp_order` as `c` ON `a`.`order_id` = `c`.`order_id`
JOIN `sp_user` as `b` ON `c`.`user_id`=`b`.`id`
JOIN `sp_invoice_stat` as `d` ON `a`.`istat_code` = `d`.`istat_code`
JOIN `sp_number` as `e` ON `a`.`number_id`=`e`.`number_id`
JOIN `sp_p_product` as `f` ON `a`.`product_id`=`f`.`product_id`
JOIN `sp_order_type` as `g` ON `c`.`otype_code`=`g`.`otype_code`
JOIN `sp_provider` as `h` ON `h`.`provider_id`=`f`.`provider_id`
WHERE `a`.`invoice_id` = '739'
ORDER BY `a`.`invoice_date` DESC 
 Execution Time:0.00018095970153809

SELECT *
FROM `sp_invoice` as `a`
JOIN `sp_order` as `c` ON `a`.`order_id` = `c`.`order_id`
JOIN `sp_user` as `b` ON `c`.`user_id`=`b`.`id`
JOIN `sp_invoice_stat` as `d` ON `a`.`istat_code` = `d`.`istat_code`
JOIN `sp_number` as `e` ON `a`.`number_id`=`e`.`number_id`
JOIN `sp_p_product` as `f` ON `a`.`product_id`=`f`.`product_id`
JOIN `sp_order_type` as `g` ON `c`.`otype_code`=`g`.`otype_code`
JOIN `sp_provider` as `h` ON `h`.`provider_id`=`f`.`provider_id`
WHERE `a`.`invoice_id` = '739'
ORDER BY `a`.`invoice_date` DESC 
 Execution Time:0.00014615058898926

JOIN `sp_user` as `b` ON `a`.`user_id`=`b`.`id`
JOIN `sp_invoice` as `c` ON `a`.`order_id` = `c`.`order_id`
JOIN `sp_invoice_stat` as `d` ON `c`.`istat_code` = `d`.`istat_code`
JOIN `sp_number` as `e` ON `c`.`number_id`=`e`.`number_id`
JOIN `sp_p_product` as `f` ON `c`.`product_id`=`f`.`product_id`
JOIN `sp_order_type` as `g` ON `a`.`otype_code`=`g`.`otype_code`
JOIN `sp_provider` as `h` ON `h`.`provider_id`=`f`.`provider_id`
WHERE `a`.`user_id` = '7'
ORDER BY `a`.`order_date` DESC
 LIMIT 10 
 Execution Time:9.8943710327148E-5

SELECT *
FROM `sp_order` as `a`
JOIN `sp_user` as `b` ON `a`.`user_id`=`b`.`id`
JOIN `sp_invoice` as `c` ON `a`.`order_id` = `c`.`order_id`
JOIN `sp_invoice_stat` as `d` ON `c`.`istat_code` = `d`.`istat_code`
JOIN `sp_number` as `e` ON `c`.`number_id`=`e`.`number_id`
JOIN `sp_p_product` as `f` ON `c`.`product_id`=`f`.`product_id`
JOIN `sp_order_type` as `g` ON `a`.`otype_code`=`g`.`otype_code`
JOIN `sp_provider` as `h` ON `h`.`provider_id`=`f`.`provider_id`
ORDER BY `a`.`order_date` DESC 
 Execution Time:0.00096702575683594

SELECT *
FROM `sp_order` as `a`
JOIN `sp_user` as `b` ON `a`.`user_id`=`b`.`id`
JOIN `sp_invoice` as `c` ON `a`.`order_id` = `c`.`order_id`
JOIN `sp_invoice_stat` as `d` ON `c`.`istat_code` = `d`.`istat_code`
JOIN `sp_number` as `e` ON `c`.`number_id`=`e`.`number_id`
JOIN `sp_p_product` as `f` ON `c`.`product_id`=`f`.`product_id`
JOIN `sp_order_type` as `g` ON `a`.`otype_code`=`g`.`otype_code`
JOIN `sp_provider` as `h` ON `h`.`provider_id`=`f`.`provider_id`
ORDER BY `a`.`order_date` DESC 
 Execution Time:0.024378061294556
